the home poe
it like fairi dwell gnomic palac built aether dream
it tini delic love replet memori sere leav novemb lili april
it castl vanish hope dim rememb dream sad memori older delug
the dead year circl slowli solemn around low white wall cloth mystic veil unseen tear
and mani marvel stori could quaint littl old hous tell mani weird cryptic stori raven hair high pallid brow sad sweet face melancholi mien belov virginia sweet child thousand magic vision child lonesom pale gray latter year child soft happi south

everi night hollow board porch must echo footfal everi morn great rise sun must sent ray littl window bath love tress dream child mystic yellow

and know hous youth love becam hous death memori bitter tear beauti woman assail dreamer within
and last left hous mourn sought solac among star
but hous remain vision magic book thing seen dark look glass love beyond dream mortal ineff sad
